fDQloc"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="bold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jAkAfA">Experience scheduling automation for yourself!</p><p font-size="s16" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 ejxNZ">Create a Calendly account in seconds.</p><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jHdkod"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx" href="/signup"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Sign up for free</span></a></div></div></div></div><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jUioWV"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-d54a3bd1-0 gHLXBH iIduIB"><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">For todays sales teams, the CRM is the central control station. All your customer data  from inbound to outbound, expansion opportunities, and more &nbsp;is recorded in and reported from your CRM, and its important to keep yours up to date.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If youre a Microsoft office user, you also probably use their native CRM: <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://dynamics.microsoft.com/en-us/sales/overview/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Microsoft Dynamics 365 Sales</span></span></a></span>. This powerful CRM enables users to close more deals with native emailing, AI-based lead scoring, and syncing with various Microsoft 365 apps.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">And if your team uses Calendly, you can now combine scheduling automation with your Dynamics 365 data. Currently available for <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/for-enterprise"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly for Enterprise</span></span></a></span> users, the <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/integration/microsoft-dynamics"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly + Microsoft Dynamics 365 integration</span></span></a></span> unlocks new workflows and automation for your sales and marketing teams, so they can spend less time on manual admin tasks like data entry, and more time driving revenue.&nbsp;</p><div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii exBzUa button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" href="/integrations/microsoft_dynamics" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Already a Calendly user? Add Dynamics 365 now!</span></a></div><h2 id="Why-integrate-Calendly-with-Microsoft-Dynamics-365" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Why integrate Calendly with Microsoft Dynamics 365</h2><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Screenshot of how after a Calendly meeting is booked, the information is automatically sent to Microsoft Dynamics." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Screenshot of how after a Calendly meeting is booked, the information is automatically sent to Microsoft Dynamics." loading="lazy" width="937" height="665" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/41107shHYuQcO7qgFI7ixO/c392f1941a9523cde9b000f38d154d8b/Email-hero-Dynamics.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 jJotaI"><figcaption class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 bTrDZA">Instantly sync all of your crucial contact and meeting information from Calendly to Microsoft Dynamics 365. </figcaption></div></figure><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">With our Calendly + Microsoft Dynamics 365 integration, when Calendly meetings are scheduled, your invitee information and scheduled meeting information is automatically added (or updated) in your records. Additional functionality includes:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Sync leads in real-time:</b> When a Calendly meeting is booked, a lead is created with up-to-date contact information. If the lead already exists in Dynamics 365, the record is updated with Calendlys most recent information.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Get insight into leads activities:</b> View upcoming and past meetings on a leads Timeline. If a meeting is rescheduled or canceled, the appointment also is updated or canceled in Dynamics 365.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Enable dynamic marketing and sales automations:</b> Always include the right team members availability or scheduling page in email campaigns and lead nurture flows. Store user-specific Calendly links in your Dynamics 365 user profile, so you dont have to manually add them to each email.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Capture form responses:</b> If you use <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/4418606043927-Getting-started-with-Routing-Forms" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly forms</span></span></a></span> to capture lead information, all submissions are added to Dynamics 365 records, too.</p></li></ul><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">These automations ensure your information is always accurate, eliminating the need for manual data entry. Save time and effort on admin tasks, so you can improve your sales process and close more deals.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK"><!-- -->Before the Microsoft Dynamics 365 and Power Automate integrations, we were going through a bunch of different routes to get our information and data where it needs to be  which wasn't super viable or scalable. With these integrations, we can set up flows to automate moving Calendly data into our Microsoft tools, and there are endless use cases to simplify our work.<!-- --></h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">Tim Francoeur</p><p class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fHWosc">Sales &amp; class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/pricing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendlys Enterprise plan</span></span></a></span>, and is enabled by <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/power-platform/products/power-automate" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Microsofts Power Automate</span></span></a></span>, so you also need to be on one of the following plans:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://dynamics.microsoft.com/en-us/sales/pricing/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Microsoft Dynamics 365 Sales Enterprise plan</span></span></a></span> or higher</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">OR <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://dynamics.microsoft.com/en-us/sales/pricing/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Microsoft Dynamics 365 Sales Professional</span></span></a></span> with an added <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://powerautomate.microsoft.com/en-us/pricing/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Power Automate plan</span></span></a></span></p></li></ul><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="/help/hc/en-us/articles/14939008641303" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Learn more about setting up the Dynamics 365 integration</span></span></a></span>.</p><h3 id="How-to-connect-the-Dynamics-365-integration" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">How to connect the Dynamics 365 integration</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Follow the simple steps below to get started with Calendlys Dynamics 365 integration.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Please note: When connecting Calendly to a Dynamics 365 account, users must have Create permission to add and update records within the account. Users also must be an Owner or Admin of their Calendly account to configure this integration.</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Go to your Integrations page and select Microsoft Dynamics 365. Youll be taken to Microsoft Power Automate to configure the Dynamics 365 integration.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Log in to your Power Automate account directly, then navigate to the Templates menu.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Search the Templates menu for "Calendly" to find our pre-built templates, and select the template you wish to use.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Next, connect your Dynamics 365 and Calendly accounts. To connect your Calendly account, return to your Integrations page, select API and webhooks, then Get a token now (or Generate New Token). Name, authenticate, and copy the token.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Return to Power Automate, name the connection and insert your token, then select Create. At this point, youre ready to use the template. Itll appear under My Flows.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Customize the automation to fit your use case by adding or removing any of the steps in the template.</p></li></ol><div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii exBzUa button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" href="/integrations/microsoft_dynamics" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Already a Calendly user? Add Dynamics 365 now!</span></a></div><h2 id="Connect-Calendly-+-Power-Automate-to-get-more-from-all-your-Microsoft-tools" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Connect Calendly + Power Automate to get more from all your Microsoft tools</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Our Dynamics 365 integration is powered by the Calendly Connector within <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://powerautomate.microsoft.com/en-us/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Microsoft Power Automate</span></span></a></span>, which means Calendly Enterprise users now also have access to our Power Automate integration! <br><br>Power Automate is Microsofts workflow automation tool, allowing users to set up quick automations between tools and boost efficiency along the way.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">With the Calendly Connector + Power Automate, you have access to an endless number of workflows that you can set up to send Calendly data into other tools in your tech stack. Here are a few of our favorites:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Send notifications to Microsoft Teams when a new meeting is scheduled.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Send Calendly data to Power BI.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Add scheduled meetings to an Excel spreadsheet, or share in Sharepoint.</p></li></ul><h2 id="Get-connected-with-Calendlys-full-suite-of-Microsoft-integrations" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Get connected with Calendlys full suite of Microsoft integrations</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">We know how important it is that all the tools in your tech stack work well together.
